			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#x201C;Our total sales </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">in the third quarter </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">declined by 14 percent due to disruptions related to the COVID-19 pandemic,&#x201D; said Garry Ridge, WD-40 Company&#x2019;s chairman and chief executive officer. &#x201C;As a global business that operates in 176 countries around the world, each of our locations has been impacted by COVID-19 in different ways but our tribe members everywhere adapted quickly to </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">the</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> unprecedented situation </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">which</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> enabled us to </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">hold our own</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> this quarter even wh</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">ile</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> confronted </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">with</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> extremely challenging circumstances.&#x201D;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </font>

			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#x201C;I have often said that physical awareness and mental awareness</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> of our product</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> &#x2013; or said simply, making our end-users aware of our products and making them easy to buy &#x2013; is core to our continued success. COVID-19 has reinforced this lesson for me. In geographies and trade channels where our products remained easy to buy, like in e-commerce and in certain countries that were not subject to movement restrictions, we performed very well in the third quarter. However, in markets with </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">strict</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> movement restrictions in place or less developed e-commerce </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">adoption</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">, our </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">sales</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> &nbsp;w</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">ere</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> more severely impacted</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">.&#x201D;</font>

			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#x201C;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">Though the global health crisis is not over yet, I do believe that we have maneuvered through the immediate crisis very well. We have always had a very clear strategy with very clear targets enabled by an enviable culture. What this crisis has required us to do is pause, reset, and become even more laser-focused on how we will achieve our growth aspirations,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#x201D;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> concluded Ridge. </font>

			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">Net sales in the Americas </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">de</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">creased </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">5</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> percent in the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">third</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> quarter primarily due to </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">lower</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> sales of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">WD-40 Multi-Use Product in</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">Latin America</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> which decreased </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">46</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> percent compared to the prior year fiscal quarter. This decline was driven </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">by disruptions around the distribution and sales of our products </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">due to the complete lock down of most countries in the region due to the COVID-19 pandemic.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> In addition, sales in Latin America were negatively impacted due to decreased sales in Mexico from period to period as </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">a result of</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> a change </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">the Company</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> made to the distribution model for this region.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">Also contributing to lower sales in the Americas were decreased </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">sales in Canada </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">which declined 10 percent </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">compared to the prior year fiscal quarter due to the negative </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">impacts of COVID-19</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">. &nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">Partially offsetting these declines were higher sales in the United States, which increased 1 percent compared to the prior year fiscal quarter due to increased demand for cleaning products as a result of the COVID-19 pandemic.</font></p></td></tr></table></div>

			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">Net sales in EMEA decreased 27 percent in the third quarter primarily due to lower sales of WD-40 Multi-Use Product throughout the Company&#x2019;s European direct and distributor markets</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">, which declined 28 and 25 percent, respectively</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">. These decreases were </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">due to</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> disruptions related to the COVID-19 pandemic</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">Also contributing to lower sales in EMEA were decreased </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">sales of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">homecare and cleaning products which declined 45 percent </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">compared to the prior year fiscal quarter</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">. This sales decrease was primarily due to </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">sales of 1001 Carpet Fresh </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">which were significantly higher in the prior year fiscal quarter </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">due to positive impacts of digital marketing associated with the brand. </font><a name="_Hlk43619726"></a><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">Changes in foreign currency exchange rates had a</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">n</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">un</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">favorable impact on sales for EMEA when compared to the prior year quarter.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> On a constant currency basis, EMEA sales for the third quarter would have decreased to $33.8 million or 24 percent compared to the prior year fiscal quarter.</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
		<div style="width:100%"><table style="width:100%; table-layout: fixed;" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0"><tr><td style="width:18pt;"><p style="width:18pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td valign="top" align="left" style="width: 18.00pt;">
			<p style="background-color: #FFFFFF;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:0.1pt 0pt 6pt;">
				<font style="margin:0.1pt 0pt 6pt;font-family:Symbol;background-color:#FFFFFF;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;;"> &#xB7;</font>
			</p>
		</td><td style="width:0pt;"><p style="width:0pt;width:0pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td align="left" valign="top">
			<p style="background-color: #FFFFFF;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:0.1pt 0pt 6pt;">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">Net sales in Asia-Pacific decreased 5 percent in the third quarter</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> primarily due to lower sales of WD-40 Multi-Use Product in the Asia distributor market, which decreased 33 percent compared to the prior fiscal quarter. The decrease in sales in the Asia distributor market was mainly </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">due to</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> disruptions related to the COVID-19 pandemic. Partially offsetting these declines were higher sales in both Australia and China, which increased 16 and 26 percent respectively compared to the prior year fiscal quarter. </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">The increase in sales in Australia was mainly driven by </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">increased</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> demand for </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">Solvol</font><sub style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xAE;</sub><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> and </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">no</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">vac</font><sub style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xAE;</sub><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> as a result of the COVID-19 pandemic.&nbsp;&nbsp;The increase in sales in China was mainly driven by the company&#x2019;s ability</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> to resume normal operations and ship many large orders in the third quarter that had previously been delayed due to the impacts of the COVID-19 pandemic and Chinese New Year.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> Changes in foreign currency exchange rates had a</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">n</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">un</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">favorable impact on sales for Asia-Pacific when compared to the prior year quarter. On a constant currency basis, Asia-Pacific sales for the third quarter would have decreased to $16.4 million or 1 percent compared to the prior year fiscal quarter.</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
		<p style="margin:0.1pt 0pt 0.1pt 36pt;background-color: #FFFFFF;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">&#xFEFF;</font>

			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">Net sales of homecare and cleaning products increased 10 percent in the third quarter when compared to the prior year fiscal quarter. This higher level of sales was due to the increased demand for such products that has resulted from the COVID-19 pandemic. </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">The </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">homecare and cleaning products, particularly those in the United States, are considered harvest brands providing healthy profit returns to the Company and are becoming a smaller part of the business as net sales of multi-purpose maintenance products grow per the execution of the Company&#x2019;s strategic initiatives. </font></p></td></tr></table></div>

			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Dividend and Share Repurchase </font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">As previously announced, WD-40 Company&#x2019;s board of directors declared on Tuesday, </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">June </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">1</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">6</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">, 20</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">20</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> a </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">regular </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">quarterly dividend of $0.6</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">7 &nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">per share payable </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">July 31</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">, 20</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">20</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> to stockholders of record at the close of business on </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">July </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">17</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">, 20</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">20</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xFEFF;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">On June 19, 2018, the Company&#x2019;s Board of Directors approved a share buy-back plan. Under the plan, which became effective on September 1, 2018, the Company is authorized to acquire up to $75.0 million of its outstanding shares through August 31, 2020. The timing and amount of repurchases are based on terms and conditions as may be acceptable to the Company&#x2019;s Chief Executive Officer and Chief Financial Officer and in compliance with all laws and regulations applicable thereto. During the period from September 1, 2018 through </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">May 31</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">, 2020, the Company repurchased&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">268,538</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> shares at a total cost of&nbsp;$</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">46.4</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;million under this $75.0 million plan.</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">On April 8, 2020, the Company elected to temporarily suspend repurchases under its current share buy-back plan. The Company has elected this suspension in order to preserve cash while it monitors the impacts of the COVID-19 pandemic as it continues to unfold. Therefore, no </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">re</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">purchase</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">s of the Company&#x2019;s stock were transacted</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> between April 8, 2020 and May 31, 2020</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xFEFF;</font>

		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">About WD-40 Company</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0.1pt 0pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">WD-40 Company is a global marketing organization dedicated to creating positive lasting memories by developing and selling products that solve problems in workshops, factories and homes around the world. The Company markets its maintenance products and homecare and cleaning products under the following well-known brands: WD-40&#xAE;, 3-IN-ONE&#xAE;, GT85&#xAE;, X-14&#xAE;, 2000 Flushes&#xAE;, Carpet Fresh&#xAE;, no vac&#xAE;, Spot Shot&#xAE;, 1001&#xAE;,&nbsp;Lava&#xAE;</font><font style="display: inline;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">and Solvol&#xAE;. &nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0.1pt 0pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xFEFF;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0.1pt 0pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">Headquartered in San Diego, WD-40 Company recorded net sales of $423.4 million in fiscal year 2019 and its products are currently available in more than 176 countries and territories worldwide. WD-40 Company is traded on the NASDAQ Global Select market under the ticker symbol &#x201C;WDFC.&#x201D; For additional information about WD-40 Company please visit</font><font style="display: inline;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;text-decoration:underline;color:#000000;">http://www.wd40company.com</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0.1pt 0pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">

		</p>

var Show={};Show.LastAR=null,Show.showAR=function(a,r,w){if(Show.LastAR)Show.hideAR();var e=a;while(e&&e.nodeName!='TABLE')e=e.nextSibling;if(!e||e.nodeName!='TABLE'){var ref=((window)?w.document:document).getElementById(r);if(ref){e=ref.cloneNode(!0);
e.removeAttribute('id');a.parentNode.appendChild(e)}}
if(e)e.style.display='block';Show.LastAR=e};Show.hideAR=function(){Show.LastAR.style.display='none'};Show.toggleNext=function(a){var e=a;while(e.nodeName!='DIV')e=e.nextSibling;if(!e.style){}else if(!e.style.display){}else{var d,p_;if(e.style.display=='none'){d='block';p='-'}else{d='none';p='+'}
e.style.display=d;if(a.textContent){a.textContent=p+a.textContent.substring(1)}else{a.innerText=p+a.innerText.substring(1)}}}
